id='poem_sentence_4_223080_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年3月15日</a>　刘庄荪来访，仍居篆畦，编篆畦唱和诗成轴，岳祥撰序。作品：篆畦诗序。<div id='poem_1317356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>篆畦诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（至元二十二年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317356")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317356'>篆畦者，予宅西之小园也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317356_comment'></div>阆风之山，自天台华顶、天封东下，过宁海分水为雁苍，东踰岭为紫洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317356_comment'></div>二山腹背为西谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317356_comment'></div>紫洞之山逆海而上，为龙舒山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317356_comment'></div>自龙舒起为大山，曰香岩，又伏而为小山，曰花架尖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317356_comment'></div>尖北为大雾山，其里为阆风，其村为尚义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317356_comment'></div>此山周回七十里，是为雁苍、紫洞之面目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317356_comment'></div>花尖之麓引而为二，其南下为长陇，予种梅植桃之地也，曰平皋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317356_comment'></div>东骛十里而为樟海，其北下曰下泽，为予五亩所居之庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317356_comment'></div>庐当北麓两臂之阿，其右臂伸而东，旧为竹杏之陇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317356_comment'></div>其左臂自花尖大雾之閒，有小涧出焉，昔人尝名之为曲水流觞之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317356_comment'></div>水南过左臂之曲，趋于平田，田实分受其灌溉之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317356_comment'></div>有咸平间古松，偃蹇周覆百步，据左臂之曲曰篆畦，盖右臂之肘腋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317356_comment'></div>其门与松相对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317356_comment'></div>予少而喜曰：「真佳山水」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317356_comment'></div>又思为䌽衣板舆奉亲之适，二亲暇日游焉休焉，虽未树亭宇，然洼隆曲折，隐见于竹树之隙，南可以眺宁海黄溪归帆落雁之缥渺也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317356_comment'></div>东可以揽月中峰云归石室洞，西可以眺玉峰之双竦、锦屏之九叠也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317356_comment'></div>北可以思故埼天封沧海之吐吞、蓬岛镇亭神物之变化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317356_comment'></div>二亲指顾之所，颇得要领，予唯唯而退，经营其中，一手茨葺，积岁月而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317356_comment'></div>予以其行径纡馀贯穿，若篆文焉，故曰篆畦，以扁其门<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上东西南北以地里方位言。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317356_comment'></div>门于宅为东向，入门为小径，横障以桧，折而西入分为三径：一为归樵岭，陟而登也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317356_comment'></div>一为小轩三间，曰无弦琴，夹径植官梅、香杏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317356_comment'></div>其一为长径，绕堤而步，夹径植玉毬、红茶、月丹、宝相、蔷薇、金沙、酴醾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317356_comment'></div>徘徊玫瑰、锦春、月季、林禽、紫薇、八仙、海棠，下植素馨、冬萱、山姜、杜若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317356_comment'></div>俯临土谷，谷中望径侧之众芳，皆覆冒于岸，若珠璎步摇之粲翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317356_comment'></div>岸上望谷中，桃李、芙蓉、杂卉，恍与岸平，若云霞之兴于步履之下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317356_comment'></div>外环以墙，墙之外，又皆芙蓉、杨柳冬青，有谷之势焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317356_comment'></div>墙与谷合，故曰谷口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317356_comment'></div>径至此北歧而为径者二：其一折而北，又折而东，至指竹亭之南，夹径植岩红、栀子、密囿、百结、紫荆、雀李、金雀之属，又折而南，过三角畦之地，遇列桧而斜避，与长径双驰，隔以月丹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317356_comment'></div>其北则丛桃，桃有千叶、真红、粉红、合欢、碧色之异，又折而过丛桃之东，老桂之西，北为好翁亭，又折而东为橘径，又折而东，北与无弦琴之径合，而入于轩中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317356_comment'></div>由轩而西，入小廊为大亭，即好翁亭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317356_comment'></div>亭北为坛三级，下植桂，中植山榴、天竹、鹿葱、玉簪之属，上植桧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317356_comment'></div>自好翁亭而西，为小廊，入指竹亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317356_comment'></div>亭北三面为小廊，自廊北入，累级而登，为乘桴亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317356_comment'></div>亭势颇高，东南见海，其下植梅，梅有千叶、红香、黄香、绿萼、真红、粉红之别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317356_comment'></div>指竹左右，皆列桧为屏，环而合于亭之南，结为洞门以出，而达乎前月丹之径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317356_comment'></div>由乘桴而北，为小廊三间，达乎耕养堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317356_comment'></div>面列桧为障，穹然如小山，即好翁亭北之上级也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317356_comment'></div>植牡丹、芍药、柽柳、含笑、赪桐、红蕉、锦带桃、独带玉毬、千叶栀、水栀、天竹之属，中有径可环绕而行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317356_comment'></div>堂有二：斋左曰方寸地，右曰静明天：此旧所居堂西之扁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317356_comment'></div>堂既改造，移置于此，不忘旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1317356_comment'></div>由耕养而东，为小廊，南入长友亭、书味轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1317356_comment'></div>轩亭皆有复轩，前为长友，而后为书味也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1317356_comment'></div>长友北有大柑树二株，盖百年物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1317356_comment'></div>取楚颂之辞以明之，亦取其甘之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1317356_comment'></div>由其左为小廊门以出，又折而为廊三间，经归樵岭西达山亭，曰羽人台，盖台可以见东山，山有陶隐居、张少霞鍊丹之故迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1317356_comment'></div>谷口之横径，自篆畦直入，至于老樟之东，凿墙为门以出，曰山扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1317356_comment'></div>扉前有竹林，竹有黄甘、旱筀、斑筀之品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1317356_comment'></div>指竹之为指竹，其殆指此竹以名之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1317356_comment'></div>由竹林开径折而东下，临荷田为舫亭，曰燕嬉舟，右曰杨柳筏，左曰芰荷洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1317356_comment'></div>燕嬉，亦旧亭名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1317356_comment'></div>亭之西夹径植海棠，循坡西北植木笔、拒霜、辛夷、紫笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1317356_comment'></div>径形正方，与山扉之前径合，其中斑竹之林也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1317356_comment'></div>由山扉北入，植丹桂木犀中，有亭曰丹林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1317356_comment'></div>由丹林西折而北，为桧障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1317356_comment'></div>穿障为洞，又以八桧为两亭，亭左右相对，揽结而成，可蔽暑日，不假般斧，旁植棕榈、丝杉、罗汉树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1317356_comment'></div>又于两亭之间凿土为井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1317356_comment'></div>井环以小廊，穿桧为门，南出为菊畦，曰花隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1317356_comment'></div>自井北入为橘井之药圃，中外皆有径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1317356_comment'></div>径列植黄杨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1317356_comment'></div>由桧亭橘圃夹径以东，植栝松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1317356_comment'></div>东折而南，又沿桧障以东，右植蜡梅，左植白茶，为阶三级以上，即指竹亭西之桧障也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1317356_comment'></div>障外皆植梅，与乘桴亭西之梅接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1317356_comment'></div>梅间横开小径，以入指竹之右腋，又阶以升乘桴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1317356_comment'></div>虽无壮武之观，华丽之饰，然步武寻常，萦回往复，若陶朱之鱼，九岛千里也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1317356_comment'></div>此篆畦之大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1317356_comment'></div>畦创于宝祐丙辰，今三十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1317356_comment'></div>畦中花木多自旧都买致，有可慨然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1317356_comment'></div>二亲既弃世，念此先人之旧游也，不忍使榛莽之翳而斤斧之入也，葺而不废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1317356_comment'></div>世殊事异，予既不仕，以农自食，又不得安其职而乐其业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1317356_comment'></div>一觞一咏，虽不减往昔，然几嬉笑而几痛哭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1317356_comment'></div>同志刘正仲居梅林而遁于雁苍，每一过余畦一相唁也，前后唱和多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1317356_comment'></div>就中过余最久者，惟癸未留半岁，有子戚而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1317356_comment'></div>甲申春冬凡四至，今岁又为余来，穷老不相忘，来当未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1317356_comment'></div>为余写前后诗成卷轴，请予序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1317356_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1317356_comment'></div>辋川之游，惟见裴迪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1317356_comment'></div>金谷之赋，仅存潘生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1317356_comment'></div>相得之难如此，而可传者益少，岂不悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1317356_comment'></div>引笔识之，实眼暗久不能书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1317356_comment'></div>正仲之小楷精妍可爱，更二十年后，亦恐不能逮今也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1317356_comment'></div>篆畦之花残木老矣，此非可久之道，书以遗我后人，他日傥有衣食馀赀，其锓于予墓之左，以光远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1317356_comment'></div>岁在乙酉三月望日，阆风舒岳祥序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1317356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1317356'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_64_1317356_0'>⑴ 以上南北东西，以居屋之前后左右而言。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1317356_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年</a>　时岳祥已学《易》作品：晚易斋2首。<div id='poem_223638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚易斋<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223638")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>六言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223638'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223638'>百年客鬓双白，四海春风一青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223638'>百舌枝头分付，黄鹂叶底丁宁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223638'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_223638_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_223637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223637?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>六言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223637'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223637'>泳道东湖联句，正仲篆畦和篇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223637'>半世清风朗月，十年闷雨愁烟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223637'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_223637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年</a>　作五律多首，写山居情怀。作品：春日山居好十首。夏日山居好十首。秋日山居好十首。冬日山居好十首。<div id='poem_223232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223232' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223232?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春日山居好十首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223232")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223232_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223232'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223232'>春日山居好，初春草色回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223232'>小桥帘映柳，野店烛簪梅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223232'>箭茁穿沙出，兰芽带雪开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223232'>从今排日去，连月覆樽罍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223232'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223232_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_223231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223231?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223231_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223231'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223231'>春日山居好，尤佳是仲春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223231'>半开花有韵，微醉酒全真。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223231'>尧帝衣裳日，周公礼乐辰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223231'>枝头百舌子，播告太谆谆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223231'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223231_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_223230' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223230' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223230?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223230_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223230'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223230'>春日山居好，春深自向归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223230'>且看成茂实，何必恋芳菲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223230'>树合明湖隔，蒿长远径微。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223230'>风雩吾党事，试浴振春衣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223229'>柳能同燕舞，莺解代花吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223229'>有酒家闲去，无诗客莫寻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223229'>卖田强免役，何必苦劳心。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　作诗赠王如山。作品：免役未几四月二十九日总府复有仓官之命五月初二日入城告诉作一绝贻如山王监薄如山前与予别谓此别不复有相见之日矣予言得十年住山不出吾事毕矣今未两月已复会面更成惨怆矣。<div id='poem_222899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_222899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/222899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免役未几四月二十九日总府复有仓官之命五月初二日入城告愬作一绝贻如山王监簿如山前与予别谓此别不复有相见之日矣予言得十年住山不出吾事毕矣今未两月已复会面更成惨怆也</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_222899'>前时临别语堪哀，后会无期首重回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_222899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_222899'>我有巾山缘未继，半年两度入城来。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年11月1日</a>　第二孙绳祖弥月，赋诗祝之。作品：腊月朔第二孙绳祖弥月喜其与翁同十一月而又皆乙亥时也因赋以祝之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗记第二孙绳祖弥月事，似有误，诗文字必有误。）</span><div id='poem_223340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>腊月朔第二孙绳祖弥月喜其与翁同十一月而又皆乙亥时也因赋以祝之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年11月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223340")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223340_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223340'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223340'>绳祖初弥月，清晨抱见翁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223340'>颇怜头额大，兼爱月时同。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223340'>句法何时就，家声待汝洪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223340_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年3月3日</a>　叹自己不知老，游于篆畦中，因作诗。作品：百一老诗序。<div id='poem_1317357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>百一老诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（至元二十四年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317357")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317357'>应璩有《百一诗》，盖百虑而有一得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317357_comment'></div>篆畦百一，直以数计耳，然亦不无意者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317357_comment'></div>天者，万物之祖，将赋百物而不知所始，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317357_comment'></div>故先之以《老天》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317357_comment'></div>天之所以生成万物者，四时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317357_comment'></div>代谢之际，固若老焉，然元亨利贞，未尝一息间断，故继之以《四时》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317357_comment'></div>维南有极，老人星居之，见则天下寿昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317357_comment'></div>夫星之丽乎天，无不寿者，此星独以老人名，盖主天下之寿者也，故继之以《老人星》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317357_comment'></div>在天成象，星辰著焉，在地成形，山川奠焉，故继之以《老山》、《老天》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317357_comment'></div>有溪有山而后民得居之，故继之以《老人村》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317357_comment'></div>村以老名，尊德尚齿，祝以寿耇，孝敬之俗成矣，故继之以《彭祖》以下六首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317357_comment'></div>村者，四民百家之杂也，故继之以《书生》以下若干首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317357_comment'></div>民物既繁，屋庐斯有，故继之以《老屋》以下若干首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317357_comment'></div>屋庐既安，则必有玩好什物之具，故继之以《老石》以下若干首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317357_comment'></div>器用之资，材木为先，蓄不可以不久也，故继之以《老椿》以下若干首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317357_comment'></div>龙者，天之骐骥，膏泽攸溥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317357_comment'></div>马者，龙之苗裔，利用无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317357_comment'></div>养生之具，首乎足食，代步之劳，逸于安车，故继之以《老龙》以下若干首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317357_comment'></div>琐碎庶汇，荣瘁倏忽，不入品者，兹不列焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317357_comment'></div>此诗止百首，而曰百一者，以吾一老人寄于百物之中为是诗者，即其一也，庶几观者知吾不知老之将至，而乐天知命，能游戏于篆畦者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317357_comment'></div>书藏晚易斋，以授吾子云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317357_comment'></div>岁在丁亥三月上巳日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1317357_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年11月27日</a>　生日邀刘庄荪等小酌，作诗。作品：贱生之日邀正仲子堂小酌。贱生之日邀正仲子堂小酌观万堂。<div id='poem_223255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贱生之日邀正仲子堂小酌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年11月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223255")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223255'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223255'>开岁恰七十，吾衰病已频。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223255'>从今数正旦，一月有三晨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223255'>甲子添新志，乾坤寄老身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223255'>晚年方学易，此意为谁陈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　麦收时节，麦饭颇可自给，有诗写食新麦齑笋的愉快。作品：村庄麦饭齑笋有怀达善正仲帅初因寄袁仲素季厚陈用之。<div id='poem_223511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223511' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_5_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_223511'>今春幸完生，一饱万事足。<div id='poem_sentence_6_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_223511'>开奁粲纤指，解苞剥寒玉。<div id='poem_sentence_15_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_223511'>风味近瑶柱，标格荐醽醁。<div id='poem_sentence_18_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_223511'>似怜老翁馋，洗我尘一斛。<div id='poem_sentence_19_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_223511'>蜕脱成癯仙，凌空驾黄鹄。<div id='poem_sentence_20_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_223511'>吐吭出新诗，落纸攲醉墨。<div id='poem_sentence_21_223511_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　喜食新麦，作诗。似与上诗同时作。<div id='poem_223329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223329?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜食新麦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223329")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223329'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223329'>乱后归田好，残生似可延。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223329'>馀花恋馀景，新麦起新烟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223329'>𤱶浍藏科斗，园林带杜鹃。<div id='poem_sentence_4_223329'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223329_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　有田妇献水麦，作诗表感怅之情。似与上诗同时作。作品：有田妇献水麦甚美不知滹沱玉食曾有此否感怅作诗。<div id='poem_223120' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223120' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223120?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有田妇献水麦甚美不知滹沱玉食曾有此否感怅作诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223120")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223120_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223120'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223120'>牟麦未全黄，和灰熟煮香。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223120'>嚼来冰响齿，咽下露生吭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223120'>肉似鸡头韧，形疑鲎子长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223120'>食芹应配美，吾欲献君王。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223120'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223120_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　秋，为白莲寺作记，阐述对“道”的理解。作品：重建台州东掖山白莲寺记。<div id='poem_1317374' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317374' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317374?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重建台州东掖山白莲寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317374")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317374_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317374'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317374'>余童冠以应乡举，过临海、宁川两界之岭，曰桐岩，日晏则息宿于白莲庄，至此过岭，可半矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317374_comment'></div>地势稍盘礴，有民庐田舍，设馆埽庭以延纳举子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317374_comment'></div>其倚山临路，乃白莲寺之庄宇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317374_comment'></div>炊黍未熟，举子亦得而游息焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317374_comment'></div>其主庄僧颇好事，设为书肆，凡举业之所资用、学者之所宜有者，皆签揭而庋列之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317374_comment'></div>或就取而观之，无拒色，亦不为二价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317374_comment'></div>涧穷壑绝，见此小佳，余尝记之在心目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317374_comment'></div>问之居人，延袤三十里，太半白莲之所有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317374_comment'></div>余故友方沂，每与余约游东掖，惜泳道先约而长逝，余苦无仆马之资，不能一往，至今为恨事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317374_comment'></div>庚寅秋，余目暗耳聩，方欲弃笔砚、习禅观，有盖苍真逸道士叶龙起，持白莲住持景荃书，致殷勤于余，其徒众又状其寺之本末，请记其伟观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317374_comment'></div>夫东掖，江南之名山，其山有白莲、能仁二寺，白莲又其著者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317374_comment'></div>昔智者师倡法于天台，《佛陇经论》行于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317374_comment'></div>庆历初，有神照法师本如诛茅结草，椎轮而建庵，绵蕝而行道，讲誉风驰，座下云集，有众五百，遂大兹刹，声闻天朝，锡号白莲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317374_comment'></div>岁久材腐，殆不能庇风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317374_comment'></div>淳熙閒，有法英师誓新旧观，道足以化人，信足以服众，仰者如山，从者若水，白莲之誉复盛于东南，学者比之国之上庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317374_comment'></div>自经口讲指画之馀者，出游诸方，自有一种风范，人咸识之，曰：「此必自白莲来也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317374_comment'></div>丙子兵火及之，殆劫会之有终欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317374_comment'></div>岁庚辰，荃师来莅兹山，天以法师惠兹山，其意深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317374_comment'></div>师道行平实，讲演著明，精义入神，四众推服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317374_comment'></div>顾瞻砾场，若疚在己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317374_comment'></div>一念奋发，天人悲涕，阴相阳赞，不十年，一寺表里规制如旧，而高广有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317374_comment'></div>上方廉节，耆宿叶和，衣钵之倾倒不吝，帑廪之出入无私，以溥容众，以裕后人，盖愿力所至，故成此不难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317374_comment'></div>或曰：「白莲不火也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317374_comment'></div>或曰：「法英不死也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317374_comment'></div>或曰：「法英师生长于台，受业于禅林，住白莲十二年，而主天竺之席；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317374_comment'></div>荃师生长亦于台，受业于禅林，来主白莲又将十二年矣，其建兹寺又同也，其殆前后身乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317374_comment'></div>寺成而谋记笔于叶君，叶君曰：「我盖苍之观新，得记于阆风先生，吾观可以不毁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317374_comment'></div>上刹东南之望也，记毋轻属，吾试为公请之于先生，先生乐道人之善，宜必得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317374_comment'></div>方盛暑，余亦火后寓凤栖茇舍，道士之请如为己请也，道士又余故考胄子补闱时所取信公子弟也，不知诺之，吐于余口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317374_comment'></div>昔韩退之以不得至南昌滕王阁为恨，而以得载名记石为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317374_comment'></div>余于白莲也亦若是矣，遂摭其事实而书之，且历叙愿见而不得至之曲折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317374_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317374_comment'></div>余之所欲访而不得偿其志者，如天台之石桥、寒岩，亦吾州之奇观也，皆有所未暇，岂兹事分量，亦有所限哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317374_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317374_comment'></div>释老二氏之并行于世也久矣，今荃师不疑叶君之异己而托之以请记，叶君亦不以荃师为不同道而为之请，余又不以二氏之非吾道而慨然为之记，皆世俗所不能解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317374_comment'></div>知此，则可与言道矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1317374_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　生日，袁仲素以羊酒赠，因作诗奉谢。作品：生日仲素惠羊酒作此奉谢。<div id='poem_223457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>生日仲素惠羊酒作此奉谢</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223457")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_223457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223457'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223457'>去年蝶轩馈羊酒，主人怜我空无有。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223457'>座上六客皆解吟，一翁不吟开笑口。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223457'>今年病叟蚤还山，烹鸡炰鳖翁对媪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223457'>五男四妇六稚孙，更有曾孙依乳姆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223457'>往来两载总遭荒，瓦瓶聊以挹酒浆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_223457'>山蔬满盘白雪白，野橘堆饤黄金黄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_223457'>荒村得此已自足，群奴饥啄撑空肠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_223457'>忽闻棠溪有书至，袁诗陈赋两辉煌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_223457'>一松正可枯檗比，五雏真与群鸡争<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_223457'>举家病疟涉三月，一日计减一斗粮。<div id='poem_sentence_9_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_223457'>留储到此作素供，问君何为特杀生。<div id='poem_sentence_10_223457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_223457'>脏神见梦羊踏菜，便呼茗碗来祓禳。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　是年作五古长诗，回忆全家避乱雪溪、棠溪的艰险困顿。作品：次韵袁伯长寄赠之作。<div id='poem_223474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵袁伯长寄赠之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223474")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_223474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223474'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223474'>维时十月闰，收穫已登场。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223474'>朋旧喜我至，殷勤置壶觞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223474'>问我何方来，忧墨见清扬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223474'>答言辱君问，欲报不成章。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_223474'>完璞保贞吉，训猷谋善臧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_223474'>嵚岖远荆棘，瘏痡辟锋铓。<div id='poem_sentence_10_223474'>长孙病风挛，二孙鹤未昂。<div id='poem_sentence_10_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_223474'>三孙始周晬，疡垢浴兰汤。<div id='poem_sentence_11_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_223474'>曾孙客中产，敢拟门户当。<div id='poem_sentence_12_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_223474'>性命幸完免，翁媪扶笋将。<div id='poem_sentence_15_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_223474'>回首烟焰涨，搜山发窖藏。<div id='poem_sentence_16_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_223474'>家林付瓦砾，书籍罹咎殃。<div id='poem_sentence_17_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_223474'>赍粮中道绝，万事慨以慷。<div id='poem_sentence_18_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_223474'>猛兽难与群，我亦思还乡。<div id='poem_sentence_21_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_223474'>又闻来屠剡，玉石恐俱伤。<div id='poem_sentence_22_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_223474'>冒暑去雪村，故里隔一冈。<div id='poem_sentence_23_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_223474'>棠溪吾故茇，父老不相忘。<div id='poem_sentence_24_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_223474'>昔行梅未落，今憩梅再芳。<div id='poem_sentence_25_223474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_223474'>皇皇一年馀，儿孙幸成行。<div id='poem_sentence_31_223474'></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_223474_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　对避乱事再致感慨。作品：秋晚随意行涧上值老农问劳去年避乱时事。<div id='poem_223253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年</a>　作诗赠刘庄荪。作品：贻正仲。<div id='poem_223257' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223257' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_223257_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223257'>为此当心恻，诗成走递筒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223257_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223257'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223257_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年4月17日</a>　为门人董景愈养志堂作记。作品：养志堂记。<div id='poem_1317371' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317371' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317371?labeling=true' target='_blank'>养志堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（至元二十八年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317371")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317371_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317371'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317371'>赏胜者领其要，摅幽者当其机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317371_comment'></div>是故神山秀岳，假高逸以扬辉，当其机也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317371_comment'></div>朗士俊人，托遐邈而含耀，领其要也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317371_comment'></div>白乐天谓会稽为首，剡为面，沃洲、天姥为眉目，诚领其实胜之要也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317371_comment'></div>谢康乐诗曰：「暝投剡中宿，明登天姥岑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317371_comment'></div>此则溯江而上，投宿剡中，明发而登天姥，自此入天台也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317371_comment'></div>唐朱放诗曰：「月在沃洲山上，人归剡县江边」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317371_comment'></div>余尝自会稽上古剡，夜望沃洲诸山，月正在其上，则知诗人之句，诚当其摅幽之机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317371_comment'></div>今自新嵊溯源而上，至于雪溪，往往以雪得名，由戴安道始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317371_comment'></div>故其地有上下雪之分，居人皆豢龙氏之裔，雁墙翚宇，花木参错，一溪贯其中，两山如匣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317371_comment'></div>夹行而西骛，半岩为飞瀑，下为灵湫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317371_comment'></div>诸董族实居上游，以笔砚肄业者十九，世以隐德著于乡，其亦赏胜之要，摅幽之机欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317371_comment'></div>余因避丙子、己丑之乱，两至其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317371_comment'></div>夫思其人者怀其棠，爱其主者及其乌，而况两至其地乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317371_comment'></div>此余既去而不能忘情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317371_comment'></div>董生景愈作新堂于旧墟，扁曰「养志」，来请记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317371_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317371_comment'></div>斯地有德于余者也，生又学于余者也，可不与之记乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317371_comment'></div>余问生之志云何，生曰：「仆不敢僭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317371_comment'></div>昔者孔门三子各言所志，咸当其才，惟点也独言浴沂风雩之趣，翛然在事物之外，而夫子与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317371_comment'></div>仆不敢僭也，然有志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317371_comment'></div>青山以为屏案，流水以为金石，奉亲读书于是，觞宾俎友亦于是，弹琴咏诗亦于是，庶几点之万一，有以承先生之教而不愧，傥可进乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317371_comment'></div>余曰：「是足以记矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317371_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317371_comment'></div>若生者，可谓得赏胜之要、摅幽之机者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317371_comment'></div>生字绍孟，今所居属新昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317371_comment'></div>至元二十八年四月十七，阆风舒某撰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1317371_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年</a>　作诗，隐隐不忘故主，感慨生活多艰。作品：端午感怀。<div id='poem_223605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端午感怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1291年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223605")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223605'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223605'>曾饮昌阳七十三，老来大布当轻衫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223605'>豫储当采三年艾，缓计空寻六日蟾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223605'>楚俗旧时沉黍恨，唐宫此日赐衣沾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223605'>栀香满院人如玉，尚想薰风半捲帘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223605'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223605_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年</a>　作诗，感慨生活多艰。作品：十九日邻家食早麦闻之有喜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年</a>　戴表元归榆林，因致诗表元，约践前言，即同游榆林。作品：去春帅初尝约为榆林游欲烹羊酿酒为小孟尝既而仆归凤栖后帅初亦往西浙遂不果今帅初已归当践前言但同游之客达善已下世矣因黄甘便作诗以叙其怀。因黄甘人便问讯帅初。<div id='poem_223070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223070?labeling=true' target='_blank'>去春帅初尝约为榆林游欲烹羊酿酒为小孟尝既而仆归凤栖后帅初亦往西浙遂不果今帅初已归当践前言但同游之客达善已下世矣因黄甘便作诗以叙其怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1291年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223070")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223070_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223070'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223070'>戴子游西浙，藕花香满船。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223070'>因思今日日，又是去年年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223070'>杨果珍闽荔，榆林下剡川。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223070'>烹羊曾有约，已失碧桃仙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223070'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223070_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_223203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223203?labeling=true' target='_blank'>因黄甘人便问讯帅初</a><span class='authorDate'>（1291年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223203")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223203_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223203'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223203'>茇舍干戈后，班荆荐莽馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223203'>何人骑有鹤，顾我食无鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223203'>孤愤向谁说，倦游休上书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223203'>时时问甘岭，戴子近何如。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223203_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223203'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223203_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年1月</a>　胡子持、孙平叔、刘庄荪建赤城先生祠于雁苍山，岳祥作诗记之。同时建赤城书堂，岳祥为书堂长。赤城书堂，宁海乡人创办的“私立”书堂。作品：壬辰正月胡子持孙平叔刘正仲诸友于雁苍建赤城先生祠赋唐律一十韵以纪其事。<div id='poem_223383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬辰正月胡子持孙平叔刘正仲诸友于雁苍建赤城先生祠赋唐律一十韵以纪其事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223383")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_223383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223383'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223383'>句读从朱老<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：先生始从朱叟峰学。）</span>，经书本释翁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223383'>于蓝青所出，他石玉堪攻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223383'>文启吾乡秀，心知百代崇<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：先生从东坡学，有诗上之）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223383'>推尊非苟合，议论自难同<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223383'>名节道乡峻，词章淮海雄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_223383'>诸公交赞誉，此老定磨砻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_223383'>旧祀儒宫侧，新祠佛寺东。<div id='poem_sentence_6_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_223383'>开山犹别子，传钵许宗风。<div id='poem_sentence_7_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_223383'>俎豆干戈后，诗书煨烬中。<div id='poem_sentence_8_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_223383'>千年期勿坏，印印此心通。<div id='poem_sentence_9_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_223383'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_223383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_223383'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_223383_0'>⑴ 自注：后与僧惟贤游，假其书，得五经，始通大义</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_223383_0'>⑵ 自注：先生因议开五丈河，坡公异意</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_223383_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年2月16日</a>　为棠溪袁仲素兄弟广孝庵作记，阐发孔子“孝”的思想。作品：广孝庵记。<div id='poem_1317372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广孝庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（至元二十九年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317372")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317372'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317372'>奉化棠奥袁氏，昔以富润屋，今以儒美身，子弟彬彬向文学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317372_comment'></div>余以己丑夏避婺寇至其地，袁仲素季厚辟堂下榻，若久故焉，余家三百指，其至如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317372_comment'></div>时余杖策度黄甘贳贷，以给朝夕餔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317372_comment'></div>二袁向人不作难色，余以是贤之，欲载其事，附见于余集中，使有传焉，然未得其目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317372_comment'></div>暇日，行其考潘奥之墓道，有石志峙焉，乃戴帅初作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317372_comment'></div>载袁君镇行事，历叙丙子避乱，初至棠奥，袁君延至其家，聚其尊稚而处焉，然后知二袁于我礼敬之意，有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317372_comment'></div>会予明年春归凤栖茇舍，二袁移书问劳相续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317372_comment'></div>明年冬，季厚之子本奉二父命来，以潘奥广孝庵请记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317372_comment'></div>余骇其名之大，谓之曰：古不墓祭，故庵庐之制未之闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317372_comment'></div>后世以庐墓为孝，于隧外作飨亭，为岁时拜埽一席地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317372_comment'></div>其后有力者又为庵于飨亭之左近，使僧徒守之，以供焚修洒埽之役；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317372_comment'></div>又其后仕宦至将相、勋阀在宗社者，得请赐寺院为镫香之奉，其事侈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317372_comment'></div>孔子葬母于防，先返而虞，使门人视窆焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317372_comment'></div>雨至墓崩，门人后至，以墓崩告，夫子泫然流涕曰：「古不修墓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317372_comment'></div>盖责其非礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317372_comment'></div>然则，既葬而往墓，不必有守庐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317372_comment'></div>今之为庵者过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317372_comment'></div>子之曾大父之墓，有汪村之庵在焉，子之大父之墓，有潘奥之庵在焉，相去一里所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317372_comment'></div>夫以一里之间而有二庵，谓是为足以广其孝，与余知子二父之意，必不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317372_comment'></div>余闻之夫子：「生，事之以礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317372_comment'></div>死，葬之以礼，祭之以礼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317372_comment'></div>何谓也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317372_comment'></div>生孰非养也，必礼也而后谓之养；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317372_comment'></div>死孰非葬也，必礼也而后谓之葬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317372_comment'></div>葬孰非祭也，必礼也而后谓之祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317372_comment'></div>子二父于其亲也，生养死葬之礼毕矣，远矣不可追矣，惟祭也，追远之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317372_comment'></div>先儒原古酌今，为家祭礼，使大夫士皆得依仿而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317372_comment'></div>丰约惟礼，不替不昵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317372_comment'></div>余闻子之二父守是庵也，有道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317372_comment'></div>云溪之村，白石之里，有祭田焉，足以供资用，粢盛、酒醴、牲牢、脯醢于是乎出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317372_comment'></div>献侑必躬必亲，以嘏以燕，遍德锡类，使观者感动曰：「孝哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317372_comment'></div>有子如此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317372_comment'></div>夫然后副是大名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317372_comment'></div>子归而复言于二父，其以余言然乎否也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317372_comment'></div>本曰：「唯唯，谨奉教」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317372_comment'></div>至元二十九年二月既望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1317372_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年11月</a>　为宁海县学作记，正面肯定了元朝崇儒重学的实际措施，且略见颂扬之意。作品：宁海县学记。<div id='poem_1317373' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317373' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317373?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宁海县学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（至元二十九年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317373")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317373_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317373'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317373'>皇帝既一南北、郡百蛮，乃尊孔氏、隆儒术，阐文治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317373_comment'></div>京师立太学，郡置学教授，县设学教谕，凡有籍于学者，皆得免徭役，士无科举之累而务问学之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317373_comment'></div>郡岁贡一士，庶几乡举里选之意，天下之士幸矣，台郡士尤幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317373_comment'></div>比年诸路县长佐多值好文敦学之彦，加意作成，又幸上置肃政廉访一司，分命马公训监临于台，首以学校为重，既新郡学，又欲新五邑学，此非台之士尤幸者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317373_comment'></div>人谓台学固幸矣，宁海学尤幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317373_comment'></div>初，宁海学之在宋东都日，与孔子庙各奠一所，高述之颂、李庆孙之记可考已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317373_comment'></div>今学与庙合，在县治之南，岁久摧压，县丞周侯汝弼尝修治之有绪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317373_comment'></div>己丑延燎于婺寇之变，县丞孙侯天锡实提学事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317373_comment'></div>盗平民定，决意兴建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317373_comment'></div>是岁七月，作讲堂直舍，朔望行礼于其中，讲说亦不废，画宫于堵，次第修举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317373_comment'></div>明年十月，判官张侯谦以督海租，至明年七月，治中王侯英以虑囚至，皆悯丞之劳，相与劝助，于是孔子殿成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317373_comment'></div>塑圣哲坐像，位列有序，拱以仪门棂星，翼以两庑八斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317373_comment'></div>游息有亭，后土有祠，下至庖溷，莫不新整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317373_comment'></div>明年十月，廉车行部至邑，入学奠谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317373_comment'></div>礼成，顾瞻斋序，周视门庑，一物不备，公以为慊，谕诸籍儒亟完治之，此岂非宁海之学尤幸者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317373_comment'></div>嗟夫，大矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317373_comment'></div>皇帝一念之仁恕，流行变化，故海隅远邑能建立如此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317373_comment'></div>于是前教谕沈桂，见教谕朱安宅、孙均，后教谕李洧、孙缉续劝率而成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317373_comment'></div>职事诸生谋树碑纪绩，而请岳祥为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317373_comment'></div>岳祥不敢辞，乃谂于众曰：「自古一统天下之主，未有不尊孔氏、隆儒术者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317373_comment'></div>汉高提三尺剑诛秦灭项，干戈甫定，过鲁祠孔子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317373_comment'></div>秦灰既冷之后，孔壁未发之前，有此伟特，可为万世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317373_comment'></div>东都建武、有唐贞观，亦一统之时也，皆用此道，立太学，幸国子监，命名儒折衷众说，集成疏义，使学者有所趋向，岂不伟欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317373_comment'></div>是故自古一统天下之主，必尊孔氏而隆儒术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317373_comment'></div>夫一统之主必若是者，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317373_comment'></div>《六经》者，理义之统也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317373_comment'></div>理义者，人心之统也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317373_comment'></div>人心者，天下之统也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317373_comment'></div>崇经术，所以明理义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317373_comment'></div>理义明，所以正人心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317373_comment'></div>人心正，则天下之统定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317373_comment'></div>统者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317373_comment'></div>惟精惟一，允执厥中，尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武心相授受之统也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317373_comment'></div>孔子心得尧舜之统者也，格物致知，诚意、正心、修身，此孔子家传之统也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317373_comment'></div>会其有极，归其有极，极者，一统之所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317373_comment'></div>是以历代帝王必得此心之统，而后一天下之统也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317373_comment'></div>孔子之徒，儒家者流，博学审问以求其说，慎思明辨以究其归，终于笃行以践其道，不杂于异端，不惑于小知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317373_comment'></div>有天下国家者，用其说则治且安，不用则危且亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317373_comment'></div>古之圣贤，无《六经》外之人物，善乎儒者之用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317373_comment'></div>其为学，一出于孔子，其用心亦若孔子而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317373_comment'></div>居无一亩之宫，而区区欲为有天下国家者治其天下国家，抑何迂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1317373_comment'></div>然而安四海之民，而不以为泰，建万载之业，而不以为功，此帝王所以尊其师而隆其术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1317373_comment'></div>皇帝盖深得统天下之要矣，此则天下之士之幸也，岂惟一郡一县之士哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1317373_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1317373_comment'></div>一雨之云，四海皆均也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1317373_comment'></div>一叶之春，八荒皆仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1317373_comment'></div>以一郡一县之学之幸，可以知天下之学之幸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1317373_comment'></div>佥曰：「唯唯」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1317373_comment'></div>是为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1317373_comment'></div>至元二十九年十一月望日，前集英殿进士舒岳祥撰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1317373_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年</a>　受邑庠之请，升讲席，说《诗·泮水》，约在此年或其前后。作品：三月之朔邑庠请仆升讲席说诗泮水正仲用前韵纪之因次其韵。<div id='poem_223031' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223031' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223031?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三月之朔邑庠请仆升讲席说诗泮水正仲用前韵纪之因次其韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223031")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223031'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223031'>春服初成冠与童，聚观王式一衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223031'>圆冠方屦还吾道，续衽钩边见古风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223031'>投戈犹待汉符赤，藏壁不随秦火红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223031'>宁可短衣充博士，莫令城旦属司空。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223031'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223031_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年</a>　作诗，静悟平生事历，有不堪回首之叹。作品：独坐遣兴。<div id='poem_223240' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223240' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223240?labeling=true' target='_blank'>独坐遣兴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1293年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223240")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223240_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_223240_0'>① 《永乐大典》卷一四三八○题作寄子堂</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223240'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223240'>昏眼迷烟雨，修眉隐树林。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223240'>杜鹃知夜半，蟋蟀俟秋音<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作吟，据《永乐大典》改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223240'>静悟平生事，閒思万古心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223240'>嗟跎七十五，既往莫追寻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223240'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223240_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年2月</a>　仲春有诗，仍念念不忘故国。作品：无题4首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年1月15日</a>　为梅林人应瑞孙作墓志铭，其次女适岳祥弟斗祥之子子普。作品：故豸峰应君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1317377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故豸峰应君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1294年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317377")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317377_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317377'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317377'>宁海以浮溪为屏几，梅林为茵席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317377_comment'></div>自提树趋而至于清泉山，是为邑之右臂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317377_comment'></div>自法昌帽尖趋而至于岳祠白峤，是为邑之左臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317377_comment'></div>梅林居其中，宽平沃衍，可容万家，为通驿大道，旁引两臂，支分港别，达于大海，有舟航网罟之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317377_comment'></div>其隅隩深窈，环以文溪，峙以茶山，有椅桐、桧柏、楩楠、豫章、竹箭、笋茗之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317377_comment'></div>钱氏有国以来，善事上都，无甲兵之扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317377_comment'></div>时有议增赋者，邑之陈长官力争之，以去官自誓，得不加敛，故民以阜安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317377_comment'></div>梅林应氏为著姓，历宋东都二百馀年，涵养生植，族聚滋茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317377_comment'></div>靖康之变，金人之师至明而退，祸不及宁邑，梅林倚郛负郭，赀用不伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317377_comment'></div>乾、淳以后，礼乐文物被焉，彬彬焉多士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317377_comment'></div>先是，吾邑自罗公适以科第起家，为时名臣，梅林二李继之，而应族邻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317377_comment'></div>其秀者相与磨砺浸灌，质剖而文蔚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317377_comment'></div>应之宗姓，其先有著籍于昌国者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317377_comment'></div>至葺芷公，乃致身参预，故梅林之应，以胄牒中举者数人，君其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317377_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317377_comment'></div>以三百馀年之族聚，而又风之以累叶之诗书，宜世其家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317377_comment'></div>君少敏锐，志气轩昂，处事如成人，而长老反取咨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317377_comment'></div>丙子归附之初，路府倚之以定寇，从权处变，捣其巢穴，获彼渠魁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317377_comment'></div>路府欲奏官之，君力辞以免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317377_comment'></div>己丑，玉山之寇荐至，宁海军帅咨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317377_comment'></div>招集流散，分别淑慝，而全活者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317377_comment'></div>路府欲以其功再闻于上，君以劳致疾，归卧湖桥，荏苒不起矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317377_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317377_comment'></div>道固多方，权非一法，天实为之，可为浩叹！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317377_comment'></div>数必有穷，虽天亦不能亨其施也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317377_comment'></div>君讳瑞孙，字季圯，自号豸峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317377_comment'></div>曾祖筌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317377_comment'></div>祖自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317377_comment'></div>考弘初，蚤世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317377_comment'></div>君娶杨氏，故文林郎相如之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317377_comment'></div>有子四：鏶之，为伯父后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317377_comment'></div>庄，早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317377_comment'></div>安之、宓之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317377_comment'></div>女三：长适故国学生陈材应，次适故承议郎、平江府长洲县舒斗祥之子子普，次适俞可翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317377_comment'></div>孙男十：山立、山京、高、延、建、尧、淼、鑫、㞳、嵱，建为庄后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317377_comment'></div>君生于绍定辛卯二月甲戌，卒于至元己未十月乙未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317377_comment'></div>以某年某月某日，葬于湖桥之原，君所自卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317377_comment'></div>君事祖母以孝，周乡党以义，与交友以信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317377_comment'></div>凡人道之常不书，余独书其处坎陷而不失其正者，所以纪世变、悲天道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317377_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1317377'>麟之彬彬兮，以不触为仁兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317377_comment'></div>众正有邻兮，豸之毅毅兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1317377_comment'></div>以触邪为义兮，群纤投畀兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1317377_comment'></div>愤世嫉时，形于色兮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1317377_comment'></div>有志无位，空太息兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1317377_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1317377'>至元三十一年正月望日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1317377_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年</a>　是年，岳祥与王应麟、刘庄荪、陈允平唱酬于梅墟陈氏之世纶堂，辑为《世纶堂雅集诗卷》，有洛社耆英之遗意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1295&endYear=1295')">1295年</a>　陈养晦赴阆风里拜谒岳祥学诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年</a>　居乡？<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1297&endYear=1297')">1297年3月</a>　为张炎词作序。作品：山中白云序。<div id='poem_1317360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317360?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山中白云词序<span class='inlineComment2'>（元贞三年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1297年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317360")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317360_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317360'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317360'>宋南渡勋王之裔子玉田张君，自社稷变置，凌烟废堕，落魄纵饮，北游燕蓟，上公车，登承明有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317360_comment'></div>一日，思江南菰米莼丝，慨然襆被而归，不入古杭，扁舟浙水东西，为漫浪游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317360_comment'></div>散囊中千金，装吴江楚岸枫丹苇白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317360_comment'></div>一奚童负锦囊自随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317360_comment'></div>诗有姜尧章深婉之风，词有周清真雅丽之思，画有赵子固潇洒之意，未脱承平公子故态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317360_comment'></div>笑语歌哭，骚姿雅骨，不以夷险变迁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317360_comment'></div>其楚狂欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317360_comment'></div>其阮籍欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317360_comment'></div>其贾生欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317360_comment'></div>其苏门啸者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317360_comment'></div>岁丁酉三月，客我宁海，将登台峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317360_comment'></div>于其行也，举觞赠言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317360_comment'></div>是月既望，阆风舒岳祥八十岁书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1317360_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1317360'><span class='label'>按：</span>《山中白云词》卷首，彊村丛书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1317360_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1297&endYear=1297')">1297年3月3日</a>　为肖翁王应辰父子留耕堂作记，赞赏“但存方寸地，留与子孙耕”作品：留耕堂记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1297&endYear=1297')">1297年6月</a>　妻王氏墓草被焚，其墓燎为焦土，岳祥重作墓志铭。作品：故孺人王氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1317378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317378?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故孺人王氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1297年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317378")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317378'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317378'>孺人王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317378_comment'></div>王氏，台宁海之王耆奥儒家子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317378_comment'></div>其里邻西洲之郑，东苍之叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317378_comment'></div>郑由发运公霖、尚书公发，叶由丞相太傅公梦鼎，以读书科第起家，为台盛大之族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317378_comment'></div>王耆诸王，有渭翁与孺人之父处士炳，与郑、叶诸公以读书应举相往来，有闻于乡，不幸以病废，而书声不绝，吟经治史相授受也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317378_comment'></div>自此群从弟子彬彬然以贡于乡、入于学者，由公渐摩始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317378_comment'></div>然其温恭醇慎之德，月旦评所推重，三聚族多科目之士，往往捷钤交驰，人皆曰：王耆奥，今当名黄旗奥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317378_comment'></div>孺人年二十二而后归于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317378_comment'></div>蚤丧母，父病末疾，孺人一意顺奉，扶翊卧起，汤药饘粥，必亲必躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317378_comment'></div>初不忍嫁，誓老于亲旁，既而考疾稍能自支，不欲遂其不字之志，乃迟之以归我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317378_comment'></div>予亦蚤有弃去场屋之兴，是时乡长上殿撰王公定勉予就举，其书在几格，孺人取读之，谓予曰：「此君分内事，宜听公言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317378_comment'></div>己酉，予始勉出应进士举，偶滥乡试首荐，既而就省闱，鹢退而反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317378_comment'></div>予自悔此出，林壑改操矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317378_comment'></div>孺人曰：「君但张弮再进，四十不成名，为梁鸿之偕隐，未晚也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317378_comment'></div>既而再中乙卯举，遂忝丙辰科进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317378_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317378_comment'></div>孺人之言，不为无补于我矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317378_comment'></div>孺人事舅姑恭顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317378_comment'></div>先君中年多病，晚亦患风弱，一日五饭，坐起非人不支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317378_comment'></div>中夜或索饭啜，孺人烹炊调胹无倦色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317378_comment'></div>先妣安人深嘉之，抚之曰：「愿汝多男长寿也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317378_comment'></div>孺人性多容少妒，姬侍生子，抚育如己出，寒暑燥湿，一皆共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317378_comment'></div>家虽贫薄，处之裕如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317378_comment'></div>勤俭自饬，一衣十年，浣濯纫缉，至老不废女工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317378_comment'></div>中年从予宦湖浙，稍有登览之胜，自能得林下风致，逸乐不在多取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317378_comment'></div>晚归东浙，历诸名山，殆有神游之意矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317378_comment'></div>世变稍烈，予与孺人同归故山，徐入鄞、剡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317378_comment'></div>山深林寂处，虽不能无登陟艰阻，然目不见兵马盗贼之畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317378_comment'></div>无病而卒于先考妣墓庐，舆归家庭，以毕棺敛，葬于县西境新宁玺山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317378_comment'></div>婺寇作，台、剡邻境，民生荼毒，三尺之坟无不椎埋暴露，独孺人遗命子妇勿用簪珥金珠为饰，一用女冠衣帔为敛具，邻里人皆疑其太薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317378_comment'></div>既瘗，不为马鬣佳城之观，至今拳然块土，苍苔丛筱蔽其上，过者莫能指其处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317378_comment'></div>此皆孺人先识明见，善缘乐趣相与合吉，有以致此欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317378_comment'></div>始，予欲与孺人合葬于此，会丁酉夏六月，穴之左右遭融风煽焰，燎为焦土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317378_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317378_comment'></div>能免于强兵大盗之毒手，而不免于刍童牧竖之遗烬，使人痛伤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317378_comment'></div>初，予卜是穴也，自坎其旁，期他日翁媪合葬于此，今罹其变，欲开隧而观之，故役人有尚存者，启予曰：「穿矿之时，其深三仞，四面皆石，脂气如蒸炊，见底而止，燎及浮土，何伤其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317378_comment'></div>若启而观之，既惊于火，又重伤之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317378_comment'></div>予允其言而已之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317378_comment'></div>孺人长予七岁，生于宋嘉定壬申二月二十八日，卒于至元甲申七月二十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317378_comment'></div>有子五人：庭坚、仲容、仲堪、叔献、季临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317378_comment'></div>有女一人，适故直敷文阁方宗卿猷之孙应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1317378_comment'></div>孙男六人：延祖早夭，绳叟、长叟、扬叟、宏叟、颐叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1317378_comment'></div>曾孙光，曾孙女八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1317378_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1317378_comment'></div>先太夫人之言，其亦有稽于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1317378_comment'></div>前之葬也，予已濡泪为志藏于家祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1317378_comment'></div>己丑兵火失之，今续为之志，其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1317378'>山之蜿蜒兮，自狮岩腾跃偃仰直下而东驰，会而融结于传领而委蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1317378_comment'></div>卓三峰其如笔兮，峙万松之崔嵬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1317378_comment'></div>有拳斯土兮，若蛹而茧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1317378_comment'></div>溪谷回环而并包兮，俨堂隍而屏帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1317378_comment'></div>合三道而东注兮，汇于沧江之湄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1317378_comment'></div>凝青点碧隐约乎几案之外兮，若骑吏宾赞旁联而拱扈，駪駪而有仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1317378_comment'></div>龟筮协吉兮，君宜其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1317378_comment'></div>既葬而安兮，孙息蕃滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1317378_comment'></div>其中无藏兮，大盗莫窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1317378_comment'></div>胡燎延于冈兮，松薄烟飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1317378_comment'></div>尚乔木之无戕兮，毋震毋危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1317378_comment'></div>北鄞西剡人过其下兮，叹息嗟咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1317378_comment'></div>阆风先生之室之藏兮，千秋万古神物其护持。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1317378_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1297&endYear=1297')">1297年12月1日</a>　是年，岳祥为里正，因作诗。作品：十二月初一醉歌。<div id='poem_223397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十二月初一日醉歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1297年12月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223397")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_223397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223397'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223397'>常年此日正月吉，今年经闰腊月一。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223397'>岁阑喜展一月期，胜似戈挥鲁阳日。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223397'>搔头偶见鹜陈横，曝背闲看蜂衙出。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223397'>一冬妍暖三月晴，薄雪微雨麦垄青。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223397'>平皋十亩锄溉毕，明年拟取甔石赢。<div id='poem_sentence_4_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_223397'>归耕还有新权柄，向时樵长今里正。<div id='poem_sentence_5_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_223397'>弟侄推尊不敢辞，斗酒只鸡先自庆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_223397'>牧猪酿秫待诛求，卖田买钞博性命。<div id='poem_sentence_7_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_223397'>北人自好南人恶，人事纷纷天未定。<div id='poem_sentence_8_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_223397'>君不见唐任涛宋魏闲，因诗放后逢宽令。<div id='poem_sentence_9_223397_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_223397'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_223397_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1297&endYear=1297')">1297年</a>　梦有神人传帝命，授梅花城长，作诗记其事。作品：梅花书塾30章。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1298&endYear=1298')">1298年</a>　八十作诗抒感。作品：读方元善落花诗有感2首。<div id='poem_223560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读方元善落花诗有感<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1298年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223560")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223560'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223560'>为渠销瘦为渠愁，减却风流剩却羞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223560'>得雨如投碧玉井，随风似堕绿珠楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223560'>医颊髓空无处觅，返魂香断为谁留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223560'>此诗吟罢难消得，八十翁翁一笑休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223560'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223560_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_222943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_222943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/222943?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1298年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_222943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_222943'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_222943'>次第花开次第飞，总堪饮酒与吟诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_222943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_222943'>绝怜新绿光如沃，何必繁英尽在枝<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书卷五八三九引《阆风集》）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_222943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_222943'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_222943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1298&endYear=1298')">1298年2月</a>　为梅林应氏七星塘作记，表达其推利于民的思想。作品：七星塘记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1298&endYear=1298')">1298年6月6日</a>　免去里役。作品：十三日晓寒独立红茶花下。<div id='poem_223289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晓寒独立红茶花下</a><span class='authorDate'>（1298年6月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223289")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223289'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223289'>长物乌皮几，宜人白氎裘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223289'>晓霜花口噤，午雨柳绵收<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223289'>毛发匆匆变，光阴冉冉休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223289'>直须瓜芡熟，长枕卧清秋<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：予以六月初六日可替里役。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223289'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_223289'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_223289_0'>⑴ 自注：柳絮正午时飞，晴则放，阴则收。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_223289_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1298&endYear=1298')">1298年6月19日</a>　卒。卒前二日赋诗三章，卒后门人私谥文清先生。作品：天门杂咏3章。<div id='poem_222829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_222829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/222829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天门杂咏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1298年6月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_222829")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_222829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_222829'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_222829'>棋寻五老智识长，茶煮八公肌骨仙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_222829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_222829'>应是青牛遗旧迹，不知白鹿去何年<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_222829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_222829'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_222829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_222829'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_222829_0'>⑴ 清王瑞成光绪《宁海县志》卷二○引刘庄孙《舒阆风先生行状》　《舒阆风先生行状》：时八十，无疾病。一日赋《天门杂咏》，甫成三章，其一云云。此绝笔也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_222829_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='26106fe3ea4846739f945c2be01a2df4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("26106fe3ea4846739f945c2be01a2df4");'><span id='26106fe3ea4846739f945c2be01a2df4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>，32岁</div><div id='26106fe3ea4846739f945c2be01a2df4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>　就省试，不中而返。妻王氏勉之再进。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7101fae2d2ef43ab98e544376b18b2b7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7101fae2d2ef43ab98e544376b18b2b7");'><span id='7101fae2d2ef43ab98e544376b18b2b7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>，38岁</div><div id='7101fae2d2ef43ab98e544376b18b2b7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年5月24日</a>　登文天祥榜进士。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7298810bba4f4d1a9d6275448697124e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7298810bba4f4d1a9d6275448697124e");'><span id='7298810bba4f4d1a9d6275448697124e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>，44岁</div><div id='7298810bba4f4d1a9d6275448697124e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　仍在丁忧中，曾到杭州讲诗。时风之下，他人多薄诗不为。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='32db60002a144d3babe310091d2593a7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("32db60002a144d3babe310091d2593a7");'><span id='32db60002a144d3babe310091d2593a7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年</a>，56岁</div><div id='32db60002a144d3babe310091d2593a7' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>两浙镇抚大使谢堂邀岳祥留都共订诸儒所评论司马光《通鉴》，拟成一家之作，奏入经筵备讲读。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>京尹曾渊子辟岳祥为户部酒所准备差遣，时贾似道当国，以其尚气简直，不即用，径弃不顾而归。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>谢堂以银酒杯相赠，或在本年。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='875bfa2735ce4007a8eda0de2346b7dc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("875bfa2735ce4007a8eda0de2346b7dc");'><span id='875bfa2735ce4007a8eda0de2346b7dc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年</a>，56岁</div><div id='875bfa2735ce4007a8eda0de2346b7dc' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在临安期间，观十年前所书《老椿》屏。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>由京师归故里。归时，买内园绿萼香梅十株，植于篆畦。<br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年6月16日</a>　在棠溪，袁仲素、季厚兄弟为辟堂下榻，岳祥家三百指，其至如归。岳祥有感于庄周梦蝶之说，名所寓曰“蝶轩”。岳祥居蝶轩，有诗文多篇，于是集己丑后诗文若干篇，目为《蝶轩稿》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　袁氏兄弟为蝶轩架杉棚以避夏炎秋暑。作品：二十八日借居喜杉棚成。次和杉棚。<div id='poem_223130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　得王达善送赵君理诗，因次韵。作品：次达善送赵君理韵因寄畲斋陈贵白。<div id='poem_223470' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223470' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223470?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次达善送赵君理韵因寄畬斋陈贵白</a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_5_223470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_223470'>笔砚易乾涩，时时要喣濡。<div id='poem_sentence_6_223470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_223470'>井汲去泥鲋，清冽用有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_223470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_223470'>自君之往矣，我怀久不舒。<div id='poem_sentence_8_223470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_223470'>久闻畬斋君，插架富名都。<div id='poem_sentence_9_223470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_223470'>欲往鵁鶄市，读书借其居。<div id='poem_sentence_10_223470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_223470'>我曾见其文，鼎脔出帅初。<div id='poem_sentence_11_223470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_223470'>何年澄斋老，道我问其途。<div id='poem_sentence_12_223470_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　赵敏求先和岳祥诗（不存），岳祥作诗寄赠。作品：寄赵敏求。<div id='poem_223310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年10月3日</a>　岳祥携家风雪中度平坑岭入马耳峰。平坑岭在台州，属何县不明。作品：+。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年10月13日</a>　夜，又从中心岙徙独山。中心岙、独山在何县不明。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　仍在逃难途中。为屯兵尚义事作“过字韵诗”以志痛。作品：过字韵诗辱诸友联和方营度枯鄙以酬厚意偶报北兵自鸥闽回驱男女牛羊万计入蛟湖深畯出独山屯尚义由童公岭以北三日夜不休闻之惊心遂成阁笔是月十四夜对月感涕遂即前韵以纪时事奉呈诸友。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223502'>牛亡主不归，妇去蚕未卧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223502_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
