宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223337")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_223337_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_223337_0'>① 叶丞相城中别业，王梅关之故园也。丙子冬兵火满地，皆黄花耳</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223337'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223337'>亭榭随人事，江山换劫灰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223337'>邹裾前日盛，谢屐几时来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223337'>红树攲城坂，黄花上石台。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223337'>欲寻观聚赋，谁与刬蒿莱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223337_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223337'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_223337_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　仍在逃难途中。丙子避兵，以萧照山水画寄藏崇庵，虽幸存，但蹂践污损已甚，为之恻然。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　在马坡与友人王达善相遇，为其《烧痕稿》题跋，并有诗唱和。马坡属何县不明。作品：跋王达善《烧痕稿》<div id='poem_1317365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317365?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋王达善烧痕稿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_1317365")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317365'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317365'>予作尉奉川日，王达善出所作相示，目曰《不切小编》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317365_comment'></div>是后奔走东西，不知是编何在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317365_comment'></div>丙子乱后还山，偶整旧箧，是编在焉，欣然如见其面，然未知达善寓吾里之马坡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317365_comment'></div>适然相遇于坡中，数相别之日，盖十有八年矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317365_comment'></div>计其续编，当倍蓰于前也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317365_comment'></div>问之，则愀然曰：「皆燬于五月之兵火矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317365_comment'></div>出其残稿数纸，题曰「烧痕」者示予，自以追忆不全为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317365_comment'></div>予解之曰：「张武之诗才数十篇，人脍炙不绝口，是在多乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317365_comment'></div>君出语散朗绵丽，简短而舂容，是不亦珍乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317365_comment'></div>毋容与俗子较多寡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317365_comment'></div>君不见都市列肆者乎，其门巷落落，终日垂帘，啄其扃，漠然不以为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317365_comment'></div>主人徐出，盥手发函，缫藉而陈之，其直动百千万计，盖所有乃珠玉瑰异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317365_comment'></div>其东家陈其所有，拄庐充栋，标于衢，号于市，又左右顾而罔诸涂，然视其内，则妻子不免饥色，盖其所售者，康瓠窭薮之具、刍灵寓马之类而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317365_comment'></div>其直之相去，固不待较。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317365_comment'></div>然则，火后仅存，尤可珍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317365_comment'></div>君博学浸灌，精思沈郁，所作未艾，时雨至矣，烧痕复青，非所病也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1317365_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　仍在逃难途中。避兵期间，艰苦备尝，且多形诸诗文。作品：丙子兵祸自有宇宙宁海所未见也予家二百指甔石将罄避地入剡贷粟而食解衣偿之不敢以渊明之主人望于人也因读渊明《乞食》诗和韵书怀呈达善亦见达善《烧痕稿》中有《陶公乞食》《颜公乞米》二帖跋尾也。<div id='poem_223439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223439?labeling=true' id='poem_title_223439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223439'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223439'>渊明不可及，适意惟所之。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　仍在逃难途中。岁末，有诗志亡国之痛，表示坚持宋遗民立场，不事新朝。作品：新历未颂遗民感怆二首贻王达善曹季辩胡山甫戴帅初诸君皆避地客也。再和前韵答达善季辩。十月初五日重赋菊。<div id='poem_223353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_7_223404_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　仍在逃难途中。因同年黄东发赠楮衾已四年，思之，作诗欲寄。作品：往时予有湖湘之游同年黄东发提举以清江楮衾赠别藏之四年矣山房夜寒覆之甚佳乱后不治东发避地何处作此拟寄。<div id='poem_223525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_223435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆筇竹杖词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_2_223435'>四明直在海东头，我得一条长在掌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223435'>蛟龙已蜕脊骨全，色如黄玉中心坚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223435'>节围五寸茎似笔，重如铁石声铿然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_223435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_223435'>杖兮杖兮吾与尔，曾入千岩万壑里。<div id='poem_sentence_5_223435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_223435'>虎豹远遁兮魑魅不逢，走及狙公兮追及鹿子。<div id='poem_sentence_6_223435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_223435'>忽不见兮谁从，宁入水兮为龙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_223435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_223435'>或以挝马兮其毁，不逢日暮兮山空，篁竹鬼啸兮雾雨其濛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_223435_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

嵊州（嵊县）

<div class='label1' id='3c8c11e564e447cfb12c513f2f235bfb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3c8c11e564e447cfb12c513f2f235bfb");'><span id='3c8c11e564e447cfb12c513f2f235bfb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>，58岁</div><div id='3c8c11e564e447cfb12c513f2f235bfb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　避兵居剡之雪溪，有董生景愈从学。<br /></div>

-----title
浙江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8eb48d29d4bb40328d00c51e23dc9ba5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8eb48d29d4bb40328d00c51e23dc9ba5");'><span id='8eb48d29d4bb40328d00c51e23dc9ba5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>，71岁</div><div id='8eb48d29d4bb40328d00c51e23dc9ba5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　春，岳祥家及家祠毁于兵火，其为夫人王氏所写墓志铭亦毁于兵火。因浙东各地陆续发生农民暴动而流徙浙东。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年1月24日</a>　避地存思庵。存思庵在何县不明。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年4月10日</a>　避乱居某山中，育母鸡以自养。作品：寇攘之余谷五斗才易一鸡衰老多病资血味以为养求之弗可得畜二母鸡自春抱育至夏百翼不减子美生理喜而有作。<div id='poem_223567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_223567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/223567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寇攘之馀谷五斗才易一鸡衰老多病资血味以为养求之弗可得畜二母鸡自春抱育至夏百翼不减子美生理喜而有作<span class='inlineComment2'>（四月初十日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年4月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_223567")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_223567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_223567'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_223567'>昔有尸乡翁，养鸡盖阡陌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_223567'>累财千馀万，积微利自博。<div id='poem_sentence_1_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_223567'>子美居瀼西，此物尚百翮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_223567'>作诗戒宗文，墙东树笼栅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_223567'>我今山居中，生理苦迫窄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_223567'>衰年资食治，时有不速客。<div id='poem_sentence_5_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_223567'>海鱼不常储，溪蟹碎难擘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_223567'>颇欲效两翁，字鸡供口食。<div id='poem_sentence_7_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_223567'>买得双伏雌，领以一赤帻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_223567'>户外听约束，安能污案席。<div id='poem_sentence_9_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_223567'>剖坼五十卵，引哺渐开拆。<div id='poem_sentence_10_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_223567'>从兹日生生，向秋益繁息。<div id='poem_sentence_11_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_223567'>麦云行刈黄，可得二十石。<div id='poem_sentence_12_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_223567'>已知饼臛具，不假天边翼。<div id='poem_sentence_13_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_223567'>窃笑茅季伟，割烹惟一只。<div id='poem_sentence_14_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_223567'>奉亲不及宾，资生拙无策。<div id='poem_sentence_15_223567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_223567'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_223567_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
新昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7fe43254ca5f4125a51262a92f85ab31_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7fe43254ca5f4125a51262a92f85ab31");'><span id='7fe43254ca5f4125a51262a92f85ab31_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>，71岁</div><div id='7fe43254ca5f4125a51262a92f85ab31' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　因家毁于兵火，身外无余物，乃避居新昌雪溪。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='34bd19d9318c4765bb4f8694d11c9ed4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("34bd19d9318c4765bb4f8694d11c9ed4");'><span id='34bd19d9318c4765bb4f8694d11c9ed4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>，71岁</div><div id='34bd19d9318c4765bb4f8694d11c9ed4' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在新昌雪溪为董伯和寿康精舍作记。作品：寿康精舍记。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>叹国亡身世已非，作诗。作品：雪村闻鸡。<div id='poem_222961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_222961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/222961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪村闻鹃</a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31402, "宋末元初", "舒岳祥", "poem_title_222961")'>舒岳祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_222961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_222961'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_222961'>故国亡来身已非，千年犹诉不如归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_222961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_222961'>参天古木魂迷路，谁与黎侯赋式微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_222961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_222961'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_222961_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
